NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

3203

PUBLIC NOTICE
R. SUNILKUMAR, aged 25 years (Male) who is mentally retarded, son of M. Ravikumar, born on 24th July 1989,
residing at 38/6, T.P. Koil Street, Triplicane, Chennai-600 005, shall henceforth be known as R.K. SUNIL KAARTHICKEYAN.
Chennai,
13th October 2014.

M. RAVIKUMAR
(Father.)

Mr. R. Arunraj was born as a male child of C. RAJENDRAN on 3rd June 1989 residing at 55/28, Kuthrath Ali Makkan
Street, Dr. Natesan Road, Triplicane, Chennai-600 005. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been living
as a Female (reference Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS.,Mch.,MNAMS.,Dip.,NB.,Phd.,FICS., Professor Head Department of Burns,
Plastic & Reconstructive Surgery, GOVERNMENT MEDICAL COLLEGE HOSPITAL, CHENNAI-600 010.) the through clinical
Examination under Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS., Mch., MNAMS., Dip., NB., Phd., FICS., Shows that I could be treated as a
Female. R. ARUNRAJ shall be known as R. ANUSHRI.
Chennai,
17th October 2014.

R. ARUNRAJ.

K. REKHA, a Female child born to P.K. Kaliyamoorthy on 19th October 1990 residing at No. 84, Balavinayakar Koil
Street, Saraswathi Nagar, Lakshmipuram, Chennai, has been living as a Male after an elaborate sexual
reassignment surgery by Dr. Sukit Worathamrong, Plastic and Reconstructive Surgeon, Yanhee International Hospital.
The same was examined and certified by Dr. V. Jayaraman, Former Professor of Plastic Surgery,
Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai, Reg.No.32070. By this, I may be treated as a Male and shall henceforth be
known as K. GOWTHAM SUBRAMANIYAM.
Chennai,

K. REKHA.

17th October 2014.

Mr. T. PATTIVEL was born as a male child of Mr. K. THURAIYAN on 20th April 1984 residing at No. 11/3, 2nd ward,
Old Ayakudi Post, Palani Taluk, Dindigul-624 613. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery, she has been living as
a female (Reference Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, MS.,Mch.,MNAMS.,Dip.,NB.,Phd.,FICS., Professor Head Department of Burns,
Plastic & Reconstructive Surgery, GOVERNMENT MEDICAL COLLEGE HOSPITAL, Chennai-600 010) the through clinical
examination under Dr. V. JAYARAMAN, Ms.,Mch.,MNAMS.,Dip.,NB.,Phd.,FICS., shows that I could be treated as a Female,
T. PATTIVEL shall be known as T. JENNIFER.
Chennai,
17th October 2014.

T. PATTIVEL.
